<script>
  !(function () {
    var analytics = (window.analytics = window.analytics || [])
    if (!analytics.initialize)
      if (analytics.invoked)
        window.console &&
          console.error &&
          console.error('Segment snippet included twice.')
      else {
        analytics.invoked = !0
        analytics.methods = [
          'trackSubmit',
          'trackClick',
          'trackLink',
          'trackForm',
          'pageview',
          'identify',
          'reset',
          'group',
          'track',
          'ready',
          'alias',
          'debug',
          'page',
          'once',
          'off',
          'on',
          'addSourceMiddleware',
          'addIntegrationMiddleware',
          'setAnonymousId',
          'addDestinationMiddleware',
        ]
        analytics.factory = function (e) {
          return function () {
            var t = Array.prototype.slice.call(arguments)
            t.unshift(e)
            analytics.push(t)
            return analytics
          }
        }
        for (var e = 0; e < analytics.methods.length; e++) {
          var key = analytics.methods[e]
          analytics[key] = analytics.factory(key)
        }
        analytics.load = function (key, e) {
          var t = document.createElement('script')
          t.type = 'text/javascript'
          t.async = !0
          t.src =
            'https://cdn.segment.com/analytics.js/v1/' +
            key +
            '/analytics.min.js'
          var n = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0]
          n.parentNode.insertBefore(t, n)
          analytics._loadOptions = e
        }
        analytics._writeKey = 'TR6z9opqX5k7OCYWwJrJGceWXQKUNNQQ'
        analytics.SNIPPET_VERSION = '4.13.2'
        analytics.load('TR6z9opqX5k7OCYWwJrJGceWXQKUNNQQ')
      }
  })()
</script>




    <script data-ot-ignore>
  const TRACKING_DATA = {
    customer: {
      id: '',
      email: '',
      first_name: '',
      last_name: '',
    },
  }

  window.Tracking = {
    debug: Boolean(localStorage && localStorage.getItem('tracking.debug')),

    init() {},

    centsToMoney(cents) {
      return ((parseFloat(`${cents}`) || 0) / 100).toFixed(2)
    },

    getRandomId() {
      return Math.random().toString().substr(2, 16)
    },

    getContext() {
      const email = TRACKING_DATA.customer.email

      return email
        ? {
            externalIds: [
              {
                id: TRACKING_DATA.customer.email,
                type: 'email',
                collection: 'users',
                encoding: 'none',
              },
            ],
          }
        : {}
    },

    getTargetingCookiesAllowed() {
      const reduceQueryToObject = (object, part) => {
        const [key, ...values] = part.split(/\s*=\s*/)
        object[key] = decodeURIComponent(values.join('='))
        return object
      }
      const cookies = document.cookie
        .split(/\s*;\s*/)
        .reduce(reduceQueryToObject, {})

      const consentCookie = cookies.OptanonConsent || null
      if (!consentCookie) return true

      const consentData = consentCookie
        .split('&')
        .reduce(reduceQueryToObject, {})
      if (!consentData) return false

      const groups = consentData.groups || null
      const targetingCookieGroup = 'C0004'

      return groups ? groups.includes(`${targetingCookieGroup}:1`) : false
    },

    validate() {
      if (!this.getTargetingCookiesAllowed()) {
        console.warn('Analytics not allowed')
        return false
      }

      if (typeof window.analytics === 'undefined') {
        console.warn('Analytics not enabled')
        return false
      }

      return true
    },

    async getUser() {
      if (!this.validate()) {
        return null
      }

      return await new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
        analytics.ready(() => {
          resolve(analytics.user())
        })
      })
    },

    track(event, properties = {}) {
      if (!this.validate()) return

      this.debugTrack(event, properties)
      analytics.track(event, properties, this.getContext())
    },

    debugTrack(event, properties = {}) {
      if (!this.debug) return

      console.log(`Analytics event fired`, {
        event,
        properties,
      })
    },

    identify(userId = null, traits) {
      if (!this.validate()) return

      this.debugIdentify(userId, traits)

      if (userId) {
        analytics.identify(userId, traits)
      } else {
        analytics.identify(traits)
      }
    },

    debugIdentify(userId, traits) {
      if (!this.debug) return

      console.log(`Analytics identify fired`, {
        userId,
        traits,
      })
    },
  }

  window.onload = Tracking.init()
</script>

(function () {
  if (window.BOOMR && (window.BOOMR.version || window.BOOMR.snippetExecuted)) {
    return;
  }
  window.BOOMR = window.BOOMR || {};
  window.BOOMR.snippetStart = new Date().getTime();
  window.BOOMR.snippetExecuted = true;
  window.BOOMR.snippetVersion = 12;
  window.BOOMR.application = "storefront-renderer";
  window.BOOMR.themeName = "";
  window.BOOMR.themeVersion = "";
  window.BOOMR.shopId = 58783793307;
  window.BOOMR.themeId = 125493444763;
  window.BOOMR.renderRegion = "gcp-europe-west1";
  window.BOOMR.url =
    "https://sg.store.ui.com/cdn/shopifycloud/boomerang/shopify-boomerang-1.0.0.min.js";
  var where = document.currentScript || document.getElementsByTagName("script")[0];
  var parentNode = where.parentNode;
  var promoted = false;
  var LOADER_TIMEOUT = 3000;
  function promote() {
    if (promoted) {
      return;
    }
    var script = document.createElement("script");
    script.id = "boomr-scr-as";
    script.src = window.BOOMR.url;
    script.async = true;
    parentNode.appendChild(script);
    promoted = true;
  }
  function iframeLoader(wasFallback) {
    promoted = true;
    var dom, bootstrap, iframe, iframeStyle;
    var doc = document;
    var win = window;
    window.BOOMR.snippetMethod = wasFallback ? "if" : "i";
    bootstrap = function(parent, scriptId) {
      var script = doc.createElement("script");
      script.id = scriptId || "boomr-if-as";
      script.src = window.BOOMR.url;
      BOOMR_lstart = new Date().getTime();
      parent = parent || doc.body;
      parent.appendChild(script);
    };
    if (!window.addEventListener && window.attachEvent && navigator.userAgent.match(/MSIE [67]./)) {
      window.BOOMR.snippetMethod = "s";
      bootstrap(parentNode, "boomr-async");
      return;
    }
    iframe = document.createElement("IFRAME");
    iframe.src = "about:blank";
    iframe.title = "";
    iframe.role = "presentation";
    iframe.loading = "eager";
    iframeStyle = (iframe.frameElement || iframe).style;
    iframeStyle.width = 0;
    iframeStyle.height = 0;
    iframeStyle.border = 0;
    iframeStyle.display = "none";
    parentNode.appendChild(iframe);
    try {
      win = iframe.contentWindow;
      doc = win.document.open();
    } catch (e) {
      dom = document.domain;
      iframe.src = "javascript:var d=document.open();d.domain='" + dom + "';void(0);";
      win = iframe.contentWindow;
      doc = win.document.open();
    }
    if (dom) {
      doc._boomrl = function() {
        this.domain = dom;
        bootstrap();
      };
      doc.write("<body onload='document._boomrl();'>");
    } else {
      win._boomrl = function() {
        bootstrap();
      };
      if (win.addEventListener) {
        win.addEventListener("load", win._boomrl, false);
      } else if (win.attachEvent) {
        win.attachEvent("onload", win._boomrl);
      }
    }
    doc.close();
  }
  var link = document.createElement("link");
  if (link.relList &&
    typeof link.relList.supports === "function" &&
    link.relList.supports("preload") &&
    ("as" in link)) {
    window.BOOMR.snippetMethod = "p";
    link.href = window.BOOMR.url;
    link.rel = "preload";
    link.as = "script";
    link.addEventListener("load", promote);
    link.addEventListener("error", function() {
      iframeLoader(true);
    });
    setTimeout(function() {
      if (!promoted) {
        iframeLoader(true);
      }
    }, LOADER_TIMEOUT);
    BOOMR_lstart = new Date().getTime();
    parentNode.appendChild(link);
  } else {
    iframeLoader(false);
  }
  function boomerangSaveLoadTime(e) {
    window.BOOMR_onload = (e && e.timeStamp) || new Date().getTime();
  }
  if (window.addEventListener) {
    window.addEventListener("load", boomerangSaveLoadTime, false);
  } else if (window.attachEvent) {

<body id="ubiquiti-store-singapore" class="template-index" ><script data-ot-ignore type="text/javascript">
  window.RequestOnce = {
    _tasks: {},

    async handle(key, requestWrapper = async () => {}) {
      if (!this._tasks[key]) {
        this._tasks[key] = requestWrapper()
      }

      return await this._tasks[key]
    },
  }

  window.APP_DATA = window.APP_DATA || {
    customer: {
      id: null,
      email: null,
      beta: false
    },

    boughtItems: [
      
    ],
  }

  window.GlobalMixin = {
    data() {
      return {
        defaultLimit: {
          minimum: 0,
          maximum: 50,
        },
        variantCustomerMaxDefault: 999,
        customerProductLimits: null,
        customerEmail: APP_DATA.customer.email,
        boughtItems: APP_DATA.boughtItems,
      }
    },

    computed: {
      shopOrigin() {
        return window.Shopify.Checkout
          ? window.Shopify.Checkout.apiHost
          : window.Shopify.shop
      },

      isLoggedIn() {
        return this.customerEmail && this.customerEmail.length > 0
      },

      boughtItemsQties() {
        const qties = {}

        if (Array.isArray(this.boughtItems)) {
          for (const { sku, qty } of this.boughtItems) {
            qties[sku] = (qties[sku] || 0) + parseInt(qty)
          }
        }

        return qties
      },
    },

    methods: {
      getCartAttribute(name) {
        const attributes = CartJS.getAttributes();
        const attribute = attributes && attributes[name] ? attributes[name] : '{}';

        return JSON.parse(attribute.replace(/=>/g, ':'));
      },

      combineLimits(generalLimits = [], customerLimits = []) {
        const combined = generalLimits.map(generalLimit => {
          const found = customerLimits.find(customerLimit => customerLimit.variantId === generalLimit.variantId)

          if (found) {
            const combinedMax = parseInt(generalLimit.max) + parseInt(found.max)
            return { ...generalLimit, max: combinedMax.toString() }
          }

          return generalLimit
        })

        const customerLimitsNotAppended = customerLimits.filter(customerLimit =>
          !combined.some(x => x.variantId === customerLimit.variantId)
        )

        const mappedCustomerLimits = customerLimitsNotAppended.map(x => {
          return {
            allowOne: false,
            max: x.max,
            sku: x.sku,
            variantId: x.variantId,
          }
        })

        return [...combined, ...mappedCustomerLimits]
      },

      async getCustomerProductLimits(forceUpdate = false) {
        // Fetch customer limits
        if (!this.customerProductLimits || forceUpdate) {
          const limits = await RequestOnce.handle('product-limits', async () => {
            const response = await fetch(
              '/apps/shop-manager/api/product-limits',
              {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: {
                  'Accept': 'application/json',
                  'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                },
                body: JSON.stringify({ shop: this.shopOrigin }),
              },
            )

            return await response.json()
          })

          // If logged in - getting customer specific limits
          if (this.isLoggedIn) {
            try {
              const customerLimits = await RequestOnce.handle('customer-product-limits', async () => {
                const response = await fetch(
                  '/apps/shop-manager/api/customer-product-limits',
                  {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: {
                      'Accept': 'application/json',
                      'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                    },
                    body: JSON.stringify({ shop: this.shopOrigin, customerEmail: this.customerEmail }),
                  },
                )
                return response.json()
              })

              this.customerProductLimits = this.combineLimits(limits, customerLimits)
            } catch(e) {
              this.customerProductLimits = limits
            }
          } else {
            this.customerProductLimits = limits
          }
        }

        // Apply allowOne changes
        if (Array.isArray(this.customerProductLimits)) {
          for (const [i, limit] of this.customerProductLimits.entries()) {
            if (!limit.allowOne) continue

            const boughtQty = this.boughtItemsQties[limit.sku] || 0

            if (boughtQty < limit.qty) continue

            this.customerProductLimits[i].max = boughtQty + 1
          }
        }

        return this.customerProductLimits
      },

      async hasLimit(id) {
        const customerProductLimits = await this.getCustomerProductLimits();

        if (Array.isArray(customerProductLimits)) {
          const hasCustomerLimit = customerProductLimits.some(
            (item) => `${item.variantId}` === `${id}`,
          );

          return hasCustomerLimit;
        };

        return false;
      },

      async getVariantLimitRequiresLogin(id, sku) {
        try {
          const hasLimit = this.hasLimit(id)
          const customerProductLimits = await this.getCustomerProductLimits()
          return hasLimit && !this.isLoggedIn

        } catch (e) {
          // console.error(e)
        }

        return false
      },

      async getVariantCustomerMax(id, sku) {
        // Get customer product limit
        try {
          const customerProductLimits = await this.getCustomerProductLimits()

          if (Array.isArray(customerProductLimits)) {
            const customerVariantLimit = customerProductLimits.find(
              (item) => `${item.variantId}` === `${id}` || item.sku === sku,
            )

            if (customerVariantLimit) {
              return parseInt(customerVariantLimit.max)
            }
          }
        } catch (e) {
          // console.error(e)
        }

        return this.variantCustomerMaxDefault
      },

      /**
       * @returns {number}
       */
      async getVariantCustomerLimit(id, sku) {
        // Check customer product limit
        try {
          const requiresLogin = await this.getVariantLimitRequiresLogin(id, sku)

          if (requiresLogin) {
            return 0
          }

          const variantCustomerMax = await this.getVariantCustomerMax(id, sku)
          const boughtQty = this.boughtItemsQties[sku] || 0

          return variantCustomerMax - boughtQty
        } catch (e) {
          console.error(e)
        }

        return this.defaultLimit
      },

      /**
       * @returns {number}
       */
      async getProductQtyLimit(id) {
        // Default limit
        let _limit = { ...this.defaultLimit }
        const setLimit = (value, type = 'maximum') => {
          _limit = this.updateLimit(_limit, value, type)
        }

        // Base limit
        const baseLimit = this.getCartAttribute('quantity-limits')[id]

        if (baseLimit) {
          setLimit(baseLimit.maximum, 'maximum')
          setLimit(baseLimit.minimum, 'minimum')
        }

        // Final limit
        return _limit
      },

      /**
       * @returns {number}
       */
      async getVariantQtyLimit(id, sku) {
        // Default limit
        let _limit = { ...this.defaultLimit }
        const setLimit = (value, type = 'maximum') => {
          _limit = this.updateLimit(_limit, value, type)
        }

        // Check customer product limit
        const customerLimit = await this.getVariantCustomerLimit(id, sku)

        setLimit(customerLimit, 'maximum')

        // Final limi
        return _limit
      },

      updateLimit(limit, value, type = 'maximum') {
        value = parseInt(value)

        if (typeof value === 'number' && value >= 0) {
          const mathType = type === 'maximum' ? 'min' : 'max'

          limit[type] = Math[mathType](limit[type], value)
        }

        return limit
      },
    },
  }
  </script>

<script type="text/x-template" id="cart-product-item">
  <div class="cart-product-item" :class="{ 'read-only': readOnly }">
    <div class="item-image">
      <template v-if="url && !readOnly">
        <a :href="url">
          <img :src="image">
        </a>
      </template>
      <template v-else>
        <img :src="image">
      </template>
      <div
        class="item-image-price"
        v-show="hideDetails"
        v-html="$root.formatMoney(finalPrice)"
        v-if="!readOnly"
      ></div>
    </div>
    <div class="item-details" v-show="!hideDetails">
      <div class="item-title">
        <template v-if="url && !readOnly">
          <a :href="url">
            ${title}
          </a>
        </template>
        <template v-else>
          ${title}
        </template>
      </div>
      <div class="item-price" v-html="$root.formatMoney(finalPrice)" v-if="!readOnly"></div>
      <slot></slot>
    </div>
    <div class="item-qty-controls" :class="{ 'disabled': disabled }">
      <template v-if="quantity === 0">
        <div class="qty-control qty-cart" @click="increaseQty">
          <img class="icon icon-cart" :src="$root.asset('icon-add-to-cart.svg')">
        </div>
      </template>
      <template v-else>
        <div
          class="qty-control qty-plus"
          :class="{ 'disabled': !canIncreaseQty }"
          @click="increaseQty"
        >
          <span v-if="!readOnly">&plus;</span>
          <span v-else>&nbsp;</span>
        </div>
        <div class="qty-control qty-amount">
          <input
            maxlength="4"
            :value="localQuantity"
            @blur="updateQtyFromInput"
            @keyup.enter="updateQtyFromInput"
            :disabled="!this.state"
          >
        </div>
        <div
          class="qty-control qty-minus"
          :class="{ 'disabled': !canDecreaseQty }"
          @click="decreaseQty"
        >
          <span v-if="!readOnly">&ndash;</span>
          <span v-else>&nbsp;</span>
        </div>
      </template>
    </div>
  </div>
</script>

<script data-ot-ignore type="text/javascript">Vue.component("cart-product-item",{template:"#cart-product-item",mixins:[GlobalMixin],props:{id:Number,title:String,image:String,price:Number,finalLinePrice:Number,quantity:Number,disabled:Boolean,url:String,hideDetails:Boolean,sku:String},data(){return{cart:CartJS.cart,limit:{},isLimitEnabled:!1,cartUpdateTimeout:null,cartUpdateDelay:500,localQuantity:this.quantity}},delimiters:["${","}"],watch:{quantity(t){this.localQuantity=t}},computed:{state(){return!this.disabled&&!this.readOnly},readOnly(){const t=this.$root.getCartAttribute("quantity-hdds"),i=(()=>{const i=[];for(const a of Object.values(t))for(const{sku:t}of Object.values(a))i.some(i=>i.sku===t)||i.push({sku:t.replace(/\/auto-add$/,""),autoAdd:t.endsWith("/auto-add")});return i})().find(t=>t.sku===this.sku);return!(!i||!i.autoAdd)},finalPrice(){return this.finalLinePrice},productId(){const t=CartJS.cart.items.find(t=>t.id===this.id);return t&&parseInt(t.product_id)},canIncreaseQty(){if(this.localQuantity>=9999)return!1;if(!this.isLimitEnabled)return!0;const t=parseInt(this.limit.maximum);return this.state&&this.localQuantity<t},canDecreaseQty(){return this.state&&this.localQuantity>0}},methods:{async setLimit(){const t=(await this.$root.getCustomerProductLimits()).some(t=>t.variantId===this.id);t&&(this.limit=t,this.isLimitEnabled=!0)},updateQuantity(t,i){this.state&&(clearTimeout(this.cartUpdateTimeout),this.cartUpdateTimeout=setTimeout(()=>{CartJS.updateItemQuantitiesById({[t]:i})},this.cartUpdateDelay))},increaseQty(){this.canIncreaseQty&&(this.localQuantity++,this.updateQuantity(this.id,this.localQuantity))},decreaseQty(){this.canDecreaseQty&&(this.localQuantity--,this.updateQuantity(this.id,this.localQuantity))},updateQtyFromInput(t){const{value:i}=t.target;let a=parseInt(i);const e=parseInt(this.limit.maximum);a>e?a=e:a<0&&(a=0),a>=0&&a!==this.quantity?this.updateQuantity(this.id,a):t.target.value=this.quantity}},created(){this.setLimit()}});</script>

<script data-ot-ignore type="text/javascript">
    const designCenterModal = new Vue({
        el: '#data-center-modal-box',

        delimiters: ['${', '}'],

        data() {
            return {
                enablePopup: false,
                tagName: 'design-center',
                tags: null,
                showPopUp: false,
                sessionKey: 'design-center-popup',
                designCenterUrl: 'https://design.ui.com/login?utm_source=storepromotion&utm_medium=web&utm_campaign=freecable/'
            };
        },

        mounted() {
            if (this.tags && this.tags.includes(this.tagName) && this.sessionData() !== '1') {
                (this.enablePopup = true);
            }
        },

        watch: {
            enablePopup(enable) {
                enable && setTimeout(this.initAddToCartListener, 200);
            },
        },

        methods: {
            handleClose() {
                this.showPopUp = false;
                this.enablePopup = false;
                this.setSessionData();
                this.sendGA(false);
            },
            handleSubmit() {
                this.sendGA();
                window.open(this.designCenterUrl, '_blank');
                this.showPopUp = false;
                this.enablePopup = false;
            },
            initAddToCartListener() {
                const btn = document.getElementById("addToCart");
                btn && btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
                    this.showPopUp = true;
                });
            },
            sessionData() {
                return sessionStorage && sessionStorage.getItem(this.sessionKey);
            },
            setSessionData() {
                if (sessionStorage) {
                    sessionStorage.setItem(this.sessionKey, '1');
                }
            },
            sendGA(transfer = true) {
                if (typeof ga !== 'undefined') {
                    ga('send', 'event', 'Transfer to DesignCenter', 'Clicked', transfer ? 'yes' : 'no');
                }
            }
        }
    })
</script>

<style>#data-center-modal-box{z-index:5000;position:fixed;width:100%;height:100%;top:0;left:0;overflow-y:auto}.dc__box{position:fixed;background:#fff;animation:fadein .5s;z-index:5000;border-radius:6px;width:540px;min-height:320px;box-sizing:border-box;overflow:hidden}.dc__overlay{position:absolute;width:100%;height:100%;z-index:5000;opacity:.6;background:#000;animation:fadeinbackground .5s}.dc__box.dc__position-center{bottom:50%;right:50%;transform:translate(50%,50%);-webkit-transform:translate(50%,50%);-ms-transform:translate(50%,50%)}.dc__box.dc__box-shadow{box-shadow:0 15px 45px 0 rgba(21,23,37,.25);-webkit-box-shadow:0 0 25px rgba(0,0,0,.5)}.dc__box svg{position:absolute;top:0;right:0;margin:17px}.dc__box .header{font-size:20px;margin:0 0 23px 0}.dc__box .header span{color:#006fff}.dc__box ul{list-style-type:none;color:#6b6d76;margin:0 0 34px 0;font-size:14px;line-height:24px}.dc__box .button-container>button{padding:11px 16px;font-size:14px;line-height:18px}@keyframes fadein{from{opacity:0;-webkit-transform:translateX(50%)}}@keyframes fadeinbackground{from{opacity:0}to{opacity:.6}}@media only screen and (min-width:568px){.dc__box{padding:32px}.dc__box img{position:absolute;right:0;bottom:80px}.dc__box img.underlay{right:-30px}.dc__box .header span{display:block}.dc__box .button-container>button{margin-right:8px}}@media only screen and (max-width:568px){.dc__box{padding:32px;width:calc(100% - 40px)}.dc__box img{max-width:50vw}.dc__box img.underlay{position:absolute;left:60px}.dc__box img.overlay{position:relative}.dc__box .header{margin:0 0 16px 0}.dc__box ul{margin:0 0 24px 0}.dc__box .button-container{display:flex;flex-direction:column}}</style>
<div id="app">
      <cart-banner
        :show="isCartBannerShown"
        :cart="cart"
        :cart-preorder-items="cartPreorderItems"
        :cart-instock-items="cartInstockItems"
      ></cart-banner>
      <cart-modal
        :open="isCartModalOpen"
        :cart-accessories="appData.cartAccessories"
        :cart="cart"
        :cart-preorder-items="cartPreorderItems"
        :cart-instock-items="cartInstockItems"
        v-on:close="closeCart"
      ></cart-modal>
    </div>

    <script data-ot-ignore type="text/javascript">
      const app = new Vue({
        el: '#app',

        data() {
          return {
            appData: APP_DATA,
            isCartModalOpen: false,
            isCartBannerShown: true,
            cart: {},
            breakpoints: {
              MOBILE: 480,
              TABLET: 768,
              LAPTOP: 960,
              DESKTOP: 1200,
            },
            isMobileResolution: false,
            isTabletResolution: false,
            defaultQtyMinimum: 0,
            defaultQtyMaximum: 50,
          };
        },

        computed: {
          cartPreorderItems() {
            return this.cart.items.filter(item => {
              return item.properties.preorder === "true"
            });
          },

          cartInstockItems() {
            const filteredItems = this.cart.items.filter(item => {
              return item.properties.preorder !== "true"
            }).reverse();

            // Move these skus to the end of array
            const targetSkus = ["HDD-8TB"];
            filteredItems.forEach(item => {
              if (targetSkus.includes(item.sku)) {
                filteredItems.push(filteredItems.splice(filteredItems.indexOf(item), 1)[0])
              }
            })

            return filteredItems;
          },

          isDevDomain() {
            return this.appData.devDomains.includes(window.location.host)
          },
        },

        methods: {
          /**
           * Group GET request parameters as an object
           *
           * @returns {Object}
           */
          searchParams() {
            const paramsMap = window.location.search
              .replace('?', '')
              .split('&')
              .map(param => param.split('='));

            // Convert the params map to an object
            const params = {};

            for (const [key, value] of paramsMap) {
              params[key] = value;
            }

            return params;
          },

          /**
           * Set resolution booleans
           */
          checkResolutions() {
            const ww = window.innerWidth;

            this.isMobileResolution = ww <= this.breakpoints.MOBILE;
            this.isTabletResolution = ww <= this.breakpoints.TABLET;
          },

          /**
           * Helper method to fetch asset with typecheck
           */
          asset(key, fallback = null) {
            const asset = this.appData.assets[key];

            return typeof asset !== 'undefined' ? asset : fallback;
          },

          /**
           * Open the cart modal
           */
          openCart() {
            this.isCartModalOpen = true;
          },

          /**
           * Close the cart modal
           */
          closeCart() {
            this.isCartModalOpen = false;
          },

          /**
           * Show the cart banner
           */
          showCartBanner() {
            this.isCartBannerShown = true;
          },

          /**
           * Hide the cart banner
           */
          hideCartBanner() {
            this.isCartBannerShown = false;
          },

          /**
           * Helper method to format money
           *
           * @param {number} cents
           * @returns {string}
           */
          formatMoney(cents) {
            const money = Shopify.formatMoney(cents).split('.');
            const suffix  = money[1] === '00' ? '' : `.${money[1]}`;

            return `<span>${money[0]}</span><span class="small">${suffix}</span>`;
          },

          formatMoneySimple(cents) {
            const money = Shopify.formatMoney(cents).split('.');
            const suffix  = money[1] === '00' ? '' : `.${money[1]}`;

            return `${money[0]}${suffix}`;
          },

          /**
           * Set-up all cart related actions
           */
          initCart() {
            // Initiate CartJS
            CartJS.init(this.appData.cart, {
              'requestBodyClass': 'loading',
              'moneyFormat': 'S${{amount}}',
              'moneyWithCurrencyFormat': 'S${{amount}} SGD'
            });

            this.cart = CartJS.cart;

            // Open the cart if requested
            if (window.location.search === "?cart") {
              window.history.replaceState({}, null, window.location.pathname);
              this.openCart();
            }

            // Handle cart header menu item
            jQuery(document).on('click', '.site-header__cart-toggle', e => {
              e.preventDefault();
              this.openCart();
            });
          },

          setProductSku() {
            const { product } = this.appData;
            const { variant: variantId } = this.searchParams();
            const skuEl = document.querySelector('.product-current-sku');

            if (product && skuEl) {
              // Use the first variant by default
              let variant = product.variants[0];

              // Find the variant based on the request parameter
              const currentVariant = variantId && product.variants.find(
                variant => parseInt(variant.id) === parseInt(variantId) && variant.sku.length
              );

              if (currentVariant) {
                variant = currentVariant;
              }

              if (variant) {
                // Update the SKU
                let gen2 = new RegExp('-gen2', 'i');
                let disabled = new RegExp('-disabled', 'i');
                let standalone = new RegExp('-Standalone', 'i');
                let beta = new RegExp('-BETA', 'i');
                skuEl.innerText = variant.sku.replace(gen2, '')
                  .replace(disabled, '')
                  .replace(standalone, '')
                  .replace(beta, '-EA');
              }
            }
          },

          makeSlug(text) {
            return text.toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z0-9]+/g, '-').replace(/-$/, '').replace(/^-/, '');
          },

          getUrlParameter(sParam) {
              var sPageURL = decodeURIComponent(window.location.search.substring(1)),
              sURLVariables = sPageURL.split('&'),
              sParameterName,
              i;

              for (i = 0; i < sURLVariables.length; i++) {
              sParameterName = sURLVariables[i].split('=');

              if (sParameterName[0] === sParam) {
                  return sParameterName[1] === undefined ? true : sParameterName[1];
              }
              }
          },

          replaceUrlParam(e,r,a){
            var n=new RegExp("("+r+"=).*?(&|$)"),c=e;return c=e.search(n)>=0?e.replace(n,"$1"+a+"$2"):c+(c.indexOf("?")>0?"&":"?")+r+"="+a
          },

          /**
           * Handle [data-toggle] that toggles [data-toggle-id] elements
           */
          handleDataToggle(e) {
            const $action = jQuery(e.currentTarget);
            const targetId = $action.data('toggle');
            const $target = jQuery(`[data-toggle-id="${targetId}"]`);

            const toggleText = $action.attr('data-toggle-text');
            const toggleTextNew = $action.attr('data-toggle-text-new');
            const toggleTextTarget = $action.children('[data-toggle-text-target]').first();

            const forceOpen = typeof $action.data('toggle-open') !== 'undefined';
            const forceClose = typeof $action.data('toggle-close') !== 'undefined' && !forceOpen;

            e.preventDefault();

            if ($action.hasClass('active') || forceClose) {
              if (!forceOpen) {
                $target.removeClass('active');
                $target.stop(true).slideUp(300);
                $action.removeClass('active');
              }
            } else if (!$action.hasClass('active') || forceOpen) {
              if (!forceClose) {
                $target.addClass('active');
                $target.stop(true).slideDown(300);
                $action.addClass('active');
              }
            }

            if(!!toggleText && !!toggleTextNew && !!toggleTextTarget) {
              $action.hasClass('active') ? toggleTextTarget.text(toggleTextNew) : toggleTextTarget.text(toggleText);
            }

          },

          /**
           * Handle [data-scroll-to] that scrolls to [data-scroll-to-id] elements
           */
          handleDataScrollTo(e) {
            const $action = jQuery(e.currentTarget);
            const targetId = $action.data('scroll-to');
            const $target = jQuery(`[data-scroll-to-id="${targetId}"]`);

            jQuery('html, body').animate({
              scrollTop: $target.offset().top,
            }, 600);
          },

          /**
           * Fetch and parse a cart attribute
           *
           * @param {string} name
           * @returns {Object}
           */
          getCartAttribute(name) {
            const attributes = CartJS.getAttributes();
            const attribute = attributes && attributes[name] ? attributes[name] : '{}';

            return JSON.parse(attribute.replace(/=>/g, ':'));
          },

          /**
           * @param {boolean} forceUpdate
           * @returns {Promise<{ sku: string; max: string }[]>}
           */
          async getCustomerProductLimits(forceUpdate = false) {
            if (!this.customerProductLimits || forceUpdate) {
              const response = await fetch('/apps/shop-manager/api/product-limits', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: {
                  Accept: 'application/json',
                  'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                },
                body: JSON.stringify({ shop: Shopify.shop }),
              })

              try {
                this.customerProductLimits = await response.json();
              } catch (error) {
                console.error(error)
                this.customerProductLimits = [];
              }

            }

            return this.customerProductLimits;
          },

          getBoughtItemQtiesGroupedBySku() {
            const boughtItems = this.appData.boughtItems;
            const boughtItemQties = {};

            for (const { sku, qty } of boughtItems) {
              const oldQty = boughtItemQties[sku] || 0;

              boughtItemQties[sku] = oldQty + qty;
            }

            return boughtItemQties;
          },

          redirectToLogout() {
            if (this.isDevDomain) {
              window.location = '/account/logout'
            } else {
              window.location = `https://sso.ui.com/api/sso/v1/logout?redirect=https%3A%2F%2F${window.location.host}%2Faccount%2Flogout`
            }
          },

          redirectToLogin() {
            // Set a local storage referral url to current page
            if (localStorage) {
              localStorage.setItem('account-login-ref', location.href)
            }

            // Redirect
            location.href = 'https://sso.ui.com/api/sso/v1/shopify_login?region=sg';
          },

          /**
           * Handle login referral redirect
           *
           * @returns {void}
           */
          handleLoginReferral() {
            if (!localStorage) {
              return
            }

            // If referral exists and not on login page
            const accountLoginRef = localStorage.getItem('account-login-ref')
            const isLoginPage = location.pathname === '/account/login'

            if (!accountLoginRef || isLoginPage) {
              return
            }

            // Remove the item
            localStorage.removeItem('account-login-ref')

            // Only if on account page (after login)
            const isAccountPage = location.pathname === '/account'

            if (!isAccountPage) {
              return
            }

            // Redirect to the referred url
            window.location = accountLoginRef
          },

          recoverPreOrderItems() {
            const localStoragePreorderItems = this.appData.localStoragePreorderItems;

            if(this.appData.template == "cart") {
              window.location = '/?cart';

            } else if(localStoragePreorderItems.length) {
              const preorderItemIds = [];
              localStoragePreorderItems.forEach(item => preorderItemIds.push({
                id: item.id,
                quantity: item.quantity,
                properties: item.properties
              }));

              CartJS.addItems(preorderItemIds, {
                "success": (data, textStatus, jqXHR) => {
                  // console.log('Preorder items has been recovered');
                  localStorage.removeItem('preorderItems');
                  this.$nextTick(this.$root.openCart);
                },
                "error": (jqXHR, textStatus, errorThrown) => {
                  // console.log('Error during updateItemQuantitiesById: ' + errorThrown + '!');
                }
              });
            }
          }
        },

        created() {
          this.checkResolutions();
          this.initCart();
        },

        mounted() {
          this.setProductSku();
          this.handleLoginReferral()

          // Events
          jQuery(window).on('resize', this.checkResolutions);
          jQuery(document).on('click', '[data-toggle]', this.handleDataToggle);
          jQuery(document).on('click', '[data-scroll-to]', this.handleDataScrollTo);

          // pushState event hack
          const pushState = history.pushState;
          history.pushState = (...args) => {
            pushState.apply(history, args);

            // Custom events
            this.setProductSku();
          };

          // Check local storage and recover preorder cart items
          // and redirect to /?cart if necessary
          this.recoverPreOrderItems();
        },
      });
    </script>

      <li><div style="height: 8px"></div></li>
    </ul><div id="geoSelectApp" class="geo-select" v-show="canShow">
  <template v-if="shop && shop.origin !== currentShopOrigin">
    <a class="close" href="javascript:void(0)" @click="close">&times;</a>

    <p>Visiting us from ${geoCountry.name}?</p>

    <template v-if="hasCurrencySelect">
      <select v-model="selectedCountryCode">
        <option v-for="shopCountry in shop.countries" :value="shopCountry.code">
          ${shopCountry.name}
        </option>
      </select>

      <select v-model="selectedCurrencyCode">
        <option v-for="currency in currencySelectCurrencies" :value="currency.code">
          ${currency.code} (${currency.name})
        </option>
      </select>

      <p class="notice">*All payments can proceed only in EUR<br />(Euro) currency</p>
    </template>

    <button class="btn btn--full" @click="openShop">Browse ${shop.name}</button>
  </template>

<script data-ot-ignore type="text/javascript">

new Vue({
  el: '#geoSelectApp',

  delimiters: ['${', '}'],

  data() {
    return {
      currentShopOrigin: Shopify.shop,
      geoCountry: null,
      shop: null,
      selectedCountryCode: null,
      selectedCurrencyCode: CURRENCY.EUR.code,
      shops: [
        {
          origin: 'truff.myshopify.com',
          url: 'https://store.ui.com',
          name: 'USA Store',
          countries: [COUNTRY.US],
        },
        {
          origin: 'store-ui-canada.myshopify.com',
          url: 'https://ca.store.ui.com',
          name: 'Canada Store',
          countries: [COUNTRY.CA],
        },
        {
          origin: 'store-ui-japan.myshopify.com',
          url: 'https://jp.store.ui.com',
          name: 'Japan Store',
          countries: [COUNTRY.JP],
        },
        {
          origin: 'store-ui-mexico.myshopify.com',
          url: 'https://mx.store.ui.com',
          name: 'Mexico Store',
          countries: [COUNTRY.MX],
        },
        {
          origin: 'store-ui-india.myshopify.com',
          url: 'https://in.store.ui.com',
          name: 'India Store',
          countries: [COUNTRY.IN],
        },
        {
          origin: 'store-ui-taiwan.myshopify.com',
          url: 'https://tw.store.ui.com',
          name: 'Taiwan Store',
          countries: [COUNTRY.TW],
        },
        {
          origin: 'store-ui-europe.myshopify.com',
          url: 'https://eu.store.ui.com',
          name: 'Europe Store',
          countries: [
            COUNTRY.AT,
            COUNTRY.BE,
            COUNTRY.BG,
            COUNTRY.HR,
            COUNTRY.CZ,
            COUNTRY.DK,
            COUNTRY.EE,
            COUNTRY.FI,
            COUNTRY.FR,
            COUNTRY.DE,
            COUNTRY.EL,
            COUNTRY.ES,
            COUNTRY.HU,
            COUNTRY.IE,
            COUNTRY.IT,
            COUNTRY.LV,
            COUNTRY.LT,
            COUNTRY.LU,
            COUNTRY.NL,
            COUNTRY.PL,
            COUNTRY.PT,
            COUNTRY.RO,
            COUNTRY.SK,
            COUNTRY.SI,
            COUNTRY.SE,
            COUNTRY.CH,
            COUNTRY.UK,
          ],
        },
        {
          origin: "me.store.ui.com",
          url: "https://me.store.ui.com",
          name: "Middle East Store",
          countries: [COUNTRY.AE],
        },
      ],
      cookieKey: 'geo-select',
      canShow: false,
    }
  },

  computed: {
    hasCurrencySelect() {
      const shopOrigins = ['store-ui-europe.myshopify.com']

      return this.shop !== null && shopOrigins.includes(this.shop.origin)
    },

    currencySelectCurrencies() {
      const result = []

      if (this.hasCurrencySelect) {
        for (const { currency } of this.shop.countries) {
          if (!result.includes(currency)) {
            result.push(currency)
          }
        }
      }

      return result
    },
  },

  methods: {
    hasCookie() {
      return typeof jQuery.cookie(this.cookieKey) !== 'undefined'
    },

    setCookie(closeAction = false) {
      jQuery.cookie(this.cookieKey, closeAction ? '0' : '1', {
        expires: 30,
        path: '/',
      })
    },

    close() {
      // Set the cookie
      this.setCookie()

      // Hide the modal
      this.canShow = false
    },

    openShop() {
      if (!this.shop) {
        return
      }

      // Set the cookie
      this.setCookie()

      // Redirect
      const shopUrlParams = this.hasCurrencySelect
        ? '?' +
          [
            `refCountry=${this.selectedCountryCode}`,
            `refCurrency=${this.selectedCurrencyCode}`,
          ].join('&')
        : ''

      window.location = `${this.shop.url}${shopUrlParams}`
    },

    async initGeoCountry() {
      if (this.geoCountry) {
        return
      }

      try {
        const url = 'https://www.ui.com/api/geoip'
        const res = await fetch(url, { method: 'POST' })
        const { country_code: code, country_name: name } = await res.json()

        // Set the country as the selected country
        this.selectedCountryCode = code
        this.geoCountry = { code, name }
      } catch (e) {
          console.error('Failed to get country. ', e)
      }
    },

    initShop() {
      if (this.shop || !this.geoCountry) {
        return
      }

      for (const shop of this.shops) {
        const hasCountry = shop.countries.some(
          ({ code }) => code === this.geoCountry.code,
        )

        if (hasCountry) {
          this.shop = shop
          break
        }
      }
    },

    handleRefParams() {
      const { origin, searchParams } = new URL(location.href)
      let reloadPage = false

      // Set country
      const refCountry = searchParams.get('refCountry')

      if (refCountry) {
        jQuery.cookie('site-country', refCountry, {
          path: '/',
        })
        reloadPage = true
      }

      // Set currency
      const refCurrency = searchParams.get('refCurrency')

      if (refCurrency) {
        jQuery.cookie('site-currency', refCurrency, {
          path: '/',
        })
        reloadPage = true
      }

      // Reload the page to update content and remove parameters
      if (reloadPage) {
        window.location = origin
      }
    },
  },

  async mounted() {
    // Init data
    await this.initGeoCountry()
    this.initShop(this.geoCountry)

    jQuery(() => {
      // Handle ref parameters
      this.handleRefParams()

      // Check if modal can be shown
      this.canShow =
        !this.hasCookie() &&
        this.geoCountry &&
        this.shop &&
        this.shop.origin !== this.currentShopOrigin
    })
  },
})
</script>

</div>

  <div class="comGlobalSearch medium-up--hide">
    <form class="search one-whole" action="/search">

<script type="text/javascript">
$(() => {
  let totalWIdth = 0;
  const $mobileShopHeaderSubmenuItems = $('#mobileShopHeaderSubmenu > li');
  $mobileShopHeaderSubmenuItems.each(function() { totalWIdth += $(this).width() });

  $('.comShopHeaderSubmenu .flexslider').flexslider({
    animation: 'slide',
    controlNav: false,
    animationLoop: false,
    slideshow: false,
    itemWidth: totalWIdth / $mobileShopHeaderSubmenuItems.length,
    itemMargin: 0,
    start: $slider => {
      const { pagingCount } = $slider;
      const itemIndex = $slider.find('.comShopHeaderSubmenu__item.active').index();
      const slidePageIndex = pagingCount !== 1 ? Math.floor(itemIndex / pagingCount) : 0;

      $slider.flexAnimate(slidePageIndex);
    },
  });
});
$(window).on('resize', () => {
  const flexData = jQuery('.comShopHeaderSubmenu .flexslider').data('flexslider');

  if (flexData) {
    flexData.setup();
  }
});
</script>

<script data-ot-ignore type="text/javascript">
new Vue({
  el: '#header-mobile-menu',

  delimiters: ['${', '}'],

  data() {
    return {
      show: false,
      tmpScrollTop: 0,
      menuData: HEADER_MENU_DATA,
      selectedMenuItem: null,
      udmProAvailable: true


    };
  },

  computed: {
    selectedMenuItemType() {
      let type = '';

      if (this.selectedMenuItem) {
        const { url } = this.selectedMenuItem;

        if (url.includes('unifi')) {
          type = 'unifi';
        } else if (url.includes('operator')) {
          type = 'operator';
        } else if (url.includes('early-access')) {
          type = 'beta';
        }
      }

      return type;
    },

    selectedMenuItemIndex() {
      if (this.selectedMenuItem) {
        const { title, url } = this.selectedMenuItem;

        switch (this.selectedMenuItemType) {
          case 'unifi':
            return this.menuData.unifi.findIndex(item => item.title === title && item.url === url);

          case 'operator':
            return this.menuData.operator.findIndex(item => item.title === title && item.url === url);
        }
      }
      return -1;
    },

    selectedMenuItemTitleContent() {
      const { operatorMenuImages } = this.menuData;
      let content = '';

      if (this.selectedMenuItem && operatorMenuImages) {
        const { title, url } = this.selectedMenuItem;

        switch (this.selectedMenuItemType) {
          case 'operator':
            // Set the SVG as the content
            content = operatorMenuImages[this.selectedMenuItemIndex];
            break;

          default:
            // Set the title by default
            content = title;
        }
      }

      return content;
    },
  
    activeMenuTitle() {
      let unifiItem = this.menuData.unifi.filter(item => {
        return item.active
      })

      let operatorItem =  this.menuData.operator.filter(item => {
        return item.active
      })
      
      if(unifiItem[0]) {
        return unifiItem[0].title

      } else if(operatorItem[0]) {
        return operatorItem[0].title

      } else {
        return false
      }
    }
  },

  methods: {
    /**
     * @param {Event} e
     */
    toggleMenu(e) {
      e.preventDefault();

      this.show = !this.show;
    },

    adjustMenuStyle() {
      const headerEl = document.querySelector('.comGlobalHeader');
      const menuEl = this.$refs.menu;

      if (menuEl) {
        // menuEl.style.top = `${headerEl.offsetHeight}px`;
        menuEl.style.height = `${window.innerHeight - headerEl.offsetHeight}px`;
      }
    },

    /**
     * @param {Object} item
     */
    menuItemClick(item) {
      if (item.links.length) {
        // Set the item as active menu item
        this.selectedMenuItem = item;
        // this.evalRecommendedPageMenuItem(item);
      } else {
        // Navigate to the page
        window.location = item.url;
      }
    },

    /**
     * @param {Event} e
     */
    deselectMenuItem(e) {
      e.preventDefault();

      this.selectedMenuItem = null;
    },

    /**
     * Force hide the cart banner
     * Using direct element manipulation is a bad practice,
     * however, there is no state management yet to do it the right way
     *
     * @param {boolean} state
     */
    toggleCartBanner(state) {
      // Use the outer wrappper to not interfere with the main element styles
      const cartBannerEl = document.querySelector('.cartBanner__outer');

      if (cartBannerEl) {
        cartBannerEl.style.display = !state ? 'none' : 'block';
      }
    },

    /**
     * Recommended menu item removed when udm-pro unavailable
     * @param {Object} item
     */
    evalRecommendedPageMenuItem(item) {
      if(this.udmProAvailable === false && item.title === 'Network') {
        const links = item.links.filter(link => link.title !== 'Complete Your UniFi OS Console');
        item.links = links;
      }
    }
  },

  watch: {
    /**
     * @param {boolean} state
     */
    show(state) {
      if (state) {
        // Scroll to the top of the page
        jQuery('html, body').scrollTop(0);

        // Disable body scrolling
        this.tmpScrollTop = jQuery(window).scrollTop();
        jQuery('body').css('overflow', 'hidden');

        // Hide the banner
        this.toggleCartBanner(false);
      } else {
        // Enable body scrolling
        jQuery('body').css('overflow', 'auto');
        jQuery(window).scrollTop(this.tmpScrollTop);

        // Show the banner
        this.toggleCartBanner(true);
      }
    },
  },

  mounted() {
    // Body ready actions
    jQuery(() => {
      this.adjustMenuStyle();
    })

    // Events
    window.addEventListener('resize', this.adjustMenuStyle);
  },

  beforeDestroy() {
    window.removeEventListener('resize', this.adjustMenuStyle);
  },
});
</script><main class="wrapper main-content" role="main">

                    <a class="btn btn--simple" @click="hideNote(note.uid, 30, i)">Okay</a>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    </template>
</div>

  const udmProBannerApp = {

      container: document.getElementById('udmProBanner'),

      anchors: {
        shopBtnAnchor: document.getElementById('udmProBannerShopBtnAnchor'),

          <path d="M12.1849 0.948796C11.7733 0.948795 11.3657 1.11545 11.0665 1.44474L0.840452 12.7611C0.386674 13.2309 0.137698 13.8474 0.137698 14.5019C0.137698 15.1565 0.386673 15.7729 0.840452 16.2427L11.0685 27.5591C11.6267 28.1755 12.5785 28.2237 13.1949 27.6655C13.8113 27.1073 13.8595 26.1556 13.3033 25.5392L3.3262 14.5019L13.3033 3.46466C13.8615 2.84824 13.8133 1.8945 13.1949 1.33832C12.9057 1.0773 12.5443 0.948796 12.1849 0.948796Z" fill="#838691"/>
        </svg>
      </div>

      <div id="bannerCarousel_navRight" class="banner-carousel__nav-right">
        <svg width="14" height="29" viewBox="0 0 14 29" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">
          <path d="M1.62417 28.0532C2.03578 28.0532 2.44338 27.8865 2.74255 27.5572L12.9686 16.2409C13.4224 15.771 13.6714 15.1546 13.6714 14.5C13.6714 13.8455 13.4224 13.2291 12.9686 12.7592L2.74054 1.44286C2.18235 0.826441 1.23062 0.778252 0.614208 1.33644C-0.00220871 1.89463 -0.0503969 2.84636 0.505783 3.46277L10.4829 14.5L0.505783 25.5373C-0.0524054 26.1537 -0.00421619 27.1075 0.614208 27.6636C0.903341 27.9247 1.26476 28.0532 1.62417 28.0532Z" fill="#838691"/>
        </svg>
      </div>
    </div>

  </div>

  <div id="bannerCarousel_footer" class="banner-carousel__footer">

  </div>

<script>
  const carouselApp = {
    state: {
      currentSlide: 1,
      autoRotateInterval: null,
      autoRotateDirection: 'right',

      animationTimeout: null,
      isAnimating: false,
      touchstartX: 0,
      touchendX: 0,
    },

    elements: {
      container: document.getElementById('bannerCarousel_slidesContainer'),
      slides: document.getElementById('bannerCarousel_slides'),
      nav: document.getElementById('bannerCarousel_nav'),
      navRight: document.getElementById('bannerCarousel_navRight'),
      navLeft: document.getElementById('bannerCarousel_navLeft'),
      footer: document.getElementById('bannerCarousel_footer'),
    },

    // Get count of slides in carousel
    getSlidesCount() {
      return this.elements.slides.childElementCount
    },

    // Get width of the overflow container in carousel
    getContainerWidth() {
      return this.elements.container.getBoundingClientRect().width
    },

    handleGesture() {
      const { touchendX, touchstartX } = this.state
      const touchSlideDistance = (touchstartX - touchendX)

      if (touchSlideDistance < -50) {
        this.slideLeft(true)
      } else if (touchSlideDistance > 50) {
        this.slideRight(true)
      } else {
        this.slideTo(this.state.currentSlide, true)
      }
    },

    // Helper to slide one step left
    slideLeft(cancelInterval = false, clickEvent) {
      const { currentSlide } = this.state
      const { slides } = this.elements

      if (clickEvent && clickEvent.stopPropagation) {
        clickEvent.stopPropagation()
      }

      if (currentSlide > 1) {
        this.slideTo(currentSlide - 1, cancelInterval)
      } else {
        this.slideTo(currentSlide)
      }
    },

    // Helper to slide one step right
    slideRight(cancelInterval = false, clickEvent) {
      const { currentSlide } = this.state
      const { slides } = this.elements

      if (clickEvent && clickEvent.stopPropagation) {
        clickEvent.stopPropagation()
      }

      if (currentSlide < this.getSlidesCount()) {
        this.slideTo(currentSlide + 1, cancelInterval)
      } else {
        this.slideTo(currentSlide)
      }
    },

    // Slide to slide number - (index 1)
    slideTo(slideNum, cancelInterval = false) {
      clearInterval(this.state.animationTimeout)
      this.state.isAnimating = true

      this.state.animationTimeout = setTimeout(() => {
        this.state.isAnimating = false
      }, 800)

      if (cancelInterval) {
        clearInterval(this.state.autoRotateInterval)
      }

      const { navLeft, navRight } = this.elements

      if (slideNum === 1) {
        navLeft.classList.add('disabled')
      } else {
        navLeft.classList.remove('disabled')
      }

      if (slideNum === this.getSlidesCount()) {
        navRight.classList.add('disabled')
      } else {
        navRight.classList.remove('disabled')
      }

      this.state.currentSlide = slideNum

      const leftPos = this.getContainerWidth() * (slideNum - 1)
      this.elements.slides.style.left = `${-leftPos}px`

      this.updateActiveThumb()
    },

    // Set the static width of slides
    setSlidesWidth() {
      const { slides, container } = this.elements
      const containerWidth = this.getContainerWidth()

      this.slideTo(1)

      slides.style.width = `${containerWidth}px`
    },

    // Update thumb elements to show current active slide
    updateActiveThumb() {
      const { currentSlide } = this.state
      const { footer } = this.elements

      let i = 0
      for (const el of footer.children) {
        if (i + 1 === currentSlide) {
          el.classList.add('active')
        } else {
          el.classList.remove('active')
        }

        i += 1
      }
    },

    initSlideThumbs() {
      const { footer } = this.elements
      const indicatorHTML = `<svg width="9" height="8" viewBox="0 0 9 8" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><circle cx="4.5" cy="4" r="4" fill="#C8CAD3"/></svg>`

      for (let i = 0; i < this.getSlidesCount(); i++) {
        const el = document.createElement('button')

        el.innerHTML = indicatorHTML
        el.id = `bannerCarouselThumb_${i + 1}`
        el.classList.add('banner-carousel__thumb')

        el.addEventListener('click', () => {
          this.slideTo(i + 1, true)
        })

        footer.appendChild(el)
      }

      this.updateActiveThumb()
    },

    initInterval() {
      this.state.autoRotateInterval = setInterval(() => {
        const { currentSlide, autoRotateDirection } = this.state
        const slidesCount = this.getSlidesCount()

        if (autoRotateDirection === 'right' && currentSlide < slidesCount) {
          this.slideRight()
        } else if (autoRotateDirection === 'right') {
          this.state.autoRotateDirection = 'left'
          this.slideLeft()
        } else if (autoRotateDirection === 'left' && currentSlide > 1) {
          this.slideLeft()
        } else if (autoRotateDirection === 'left') {
          this.state.autoRotateDirection = 'right'
          this.slideRight()
        }
      }, 6000)
    },

    init() {
      const {
        container,
        slides,
        navRight,
        navLeft,
        nav,
      } = this.elements

      this.setSlidesWidth()
      this.initSlideThumbs()
      this.slideTo(1)
      this.initInterval()

      window.addEventListener('resize', this.setSlidesWidth.bind(this))
      navRight.addEventListener('click', () => this.slideRight.bind(this)(true, event))
      navLeft.addEventListener('click', () => this.slideLeft.bind(this)(true, event))

      /**
       * Record touchstart X positon
       */
      container.addEventListener('touchstart', e => {
        if (this.state.isAnimating) {
          this.state.touchstartX = null
          return
        }

        slides.style.transition = 'none'
        this.state.touchstartX = e.changedTouches[0].screenX
      })

      /**
       * Visual "drag" animation
       */
      container.addEventListener('touchmove', e => {
        if (typeof this.state.touchstartX !== 'number') {
          return
        }

        const draggedDistance = e.changedTouches[0].screenX - this.state.touchstartX
        const currentSlideLeftPos = 0 - (this.getContainerWidth() * (this.state.currentSlide - 1))

        const draggedLeftPos = currentSlideLeftPos + (draggedDistance / 2)
        const minLeftPos = 0 - (this.getContainerWidth() * (this.getSlidesCount() - 1))

        if (draggedLeftPos < 0 && draggedLeftPos > minLeftPos) {
          slides.style.left = `${draggedLeftPos}px`
        }
      })

      /**
       * Record touchend X positon and check if valid gesture for carousel slide
       */
      container.addEventListener('touchend', e => {
        if (typeof this.state.touchstartX !== 'number') {
          return
        }

        slides.style.transition = 'left .8s'
        this.state.touchendX = e.changedTouches[0].screenX
        this.handleGesture()
      })

      nav.style.display = 'block'
    },
  }

  window.addEventListener('load', () => {
    carouselApp.init()
  })
</script>

    margin-right: -32px;
    /***/

  }
